Women's Health Recommendations:

Overview Notes: Supplement with vitamin D3 5000 iu daily for 4 months then recheck your level aiming for a level of 50 to 80 ng/ml. Once you are in this range you can decrease your supplement to 1000 to 2000 iu daily.
Comment Key: ClinicalExamComment
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Nil

Men's Health Recommendations: 
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Your BMI and waist circumference are both significantly high. Weight around the abdomen is associated with an increased risk of chronic disease such as heart disease, type 2 diabetes and certain cancers. Weight around the abdomen is associated with an increased risk of chronic disease such as heart disease, type 2 diabetes and certain cancers. You want to aim for a waist circumference of 80cms or less. Continue with the dietary changes that you have made and try to start exercising.

Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Your BMI and waist circumference are both significantly high. Weight around the abdomen is associated with an increased risk of chronic disease such as heart disease, type 2 diabetes and certain cancers. You want to aim for a waist circumference of 80cms or less. Continue with the dietary changes that you have made and try to start exercising.
Comment Key: VitalsNote
Comment Value: High waist circumference and BMI, elevated BP
Special Investigation Notes: Nil
